USERMESSAGE #13
✓ TOOL RESULT
SUCCESS 
     1→/**
     2→ * Character.js — tile-based character with A* pathfinding and state machine.
     3→ * Pure JS, no Phaser dependency. Sprite/label references are set externally.
     4→ */
     5→
     6→const TILE_SIZE = 48;
     7→
     8→// ─── A* pathfinding ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
     9→
    10→function heuristic(ax, ay, bx, by) {
    11→  return Math.abs(ax - bx) + Math.abs(ay - by);
    12→}
    13→
    14→/**
    15→ * Find a path from (startX, startY) to (goalX, goalY) on a walkable grid.
    16→ * @param {boolean[][]} walkable  - walkable[row][col]
    17→ * @param {number} cols
    18→ * @param {number} rows
    19→ * @returns {Array<{tx,ty}>|null}  - list of steps NOT including start; null if no path
    20→ */
    21→function findPath(walkable, cols, rows, startX, startY, goalX, goalY) {
    22→  if (startX === goalX && startY === goalY) return [];
    23→  if (!walkable[startY]?.[startX] || !walkable[goalY]?.[goalX]) return null;
    24→
    25→  const key = (x, y) => x * 1000 + y;
    26→
    27→  const open = new Map();
    28→  const closed = new Set();
    29→
    30→  const startNode = { x: startX, y: startY, g: 0, h: heuristic(startX, startY, goalX, goalY), parent: null };
    31→  open.set(key(startX, startY), startNode);
    32→
    33→  while (open.size > 0) {
    34→    // Pick node with lowest f = g + h
    35→    let current = null;
    36→    for (const node of open.values()) {
    37→      if (!current || node.g + node.h < current.g + current.h) current = node;
    38→    }
    39→
    40→    if (current.x === goalX && current.y === goalY) {
    41→      // Reconstruct path
    42→      const path = [];
    43→      let node = current;
    44→      while (node.parent) {
    45→        path.unshift({ tx: node.x, ty: node.y });
    46→        node = node.parent;
    47→      }
    48→      return path;
    49→    }
    50→
    51→    open.delete(key(current.x, current.y));
    52→    closed.add(key(current.x, current.y));
    53→
    54→    const neighbors = [
    55→      { x: current.x + 1, y: current.y },
    56→      { x: current.x - 1, y: current.y },
    57→      { x: current.x,     y: current.y + 1 },
    58→      { x: current.x,     y: current.y - 1 },
    59→    ];
    60→
    61→    for (const n of neighbors) {
    62→      if (n.x < 0 || n.x >= cols || n.y < 0 || n.y >= rows) continue;
    63→      if (!walkable[n.y]?.[n.x]) continue;
    64→      if (closed.has(key(n.x, n.y))) continue;
    65→
    66→      const g = current.g + 1;
    67→      const existing = open.get(key(n.x, n.y));
    68→      if (existing) {
    69→        if (g < existing.g) {
    70→          existing.g = g;
    71→          existing.parent = current;
    72→        }
    73→      } else {
    74→        open.set(key(n.x, n.y), {
    75→          x: n.x, y: n.y,
    76→          g, h: heuristic(n.x, n.y, goalX, goalY),
    77→          parent: current,
    78→        });
    79→      }
    80→    }
    81→  }
    82→
    83→  return null; // no path
    84→}
    85→
    86→// ─── Character ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    87→
    88→export class Character {
    89→  /**
    90→   * @param {object} config
    91→   * @param {string}   config.name        - sprite key prefix (e.g. 'Amelia')
    92→   * @param {string}   config.label       - display name (e.g. 'Maple')
    93→   * @param {number}   config.tx          - starting tile X
    94→   * @param {number}   config.ty          - starting tile Y
    95→   * @param {boolean[][]} config.walkable - walkable grid [row][col]
    96→   * @param {number}   config.gridCols
    97→   * @param {number}   config.gridRows
    98→   * @param {object}   [config.sprite]    - Phaser sprite (set after construction)
    99→   * @param {object}   [config.nameLabel] - Phaser Text object
   100→   * @param {number}   [config.moveSpeed] - tiles per second (default 2)
   101→   */
   102→  constructor(config) {
   103→    this.name      = config.name;
   104→    this.label     = config.label;
   105→    this.sprite    = config.sprite    || null;
   106→    this.nameLabel = config.nameLabel || null;
   107→
   108→    this.tx     = config.tx;
   109→    this.ty     = config.ty;
   110→    this.prevTx = config.tx;
   111→    this.prevTy = config.ty;
   112→
   113→    this.path        = [];
   114→    this.moveProgress = 0;
   115→    this.moveSpeed   = config.moveSpeed || 2; // tiles/sec
   116→
   117→    // State: 'idle' | 'walking' | 'interacting' | 'talking'
   118→    this.action = 'idle';
   119→    this.facing = 'down';
   120→
   121→    // Wander: timer counts DOWN; engine starts wander when <= 0
   122→    this.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000; // 3–8 s
   123→
   124→    // Interaction
   125→    this.interactTimer    = 0;
   126→    this.interactTimerMax = 0; // initial duration; used by UI for progress bar
   127→    this.interactTarget   = null;
   128→
   129→    // Personality stats (0–100)
   130→    this.mood   = 100;
   131→    this.energy = 100;
   132→
   133→    // Optional dialogue driven by AI
   134→    this.currentDialogue = null;
   135→    this.dialogueTimer   = 0;
   136→
   137→    // Preset dialogue lines (used for random speech bubbles)
   138→    this.dialogue     = config.dialogue || [];
   139→    // Counts down; when it hits 0 Engine sets pendingSpeech
   140→    this.speechTimer  = 20000 + Math.random() * 20000; // 20–40 s
   141→    // Scene reads this each frame and shows a bubble, then clears it
   142→    this.pendingSpeech = null;
   143→
   144→    this.walkable  = config.walkable;
   145→    this.gridCols  = config.gridCols;
   146→    this.gridRows  = config.gridRows;
   147→
   148→    // Object interaction targeting — set by engine, cleared on arrival
   149→    this.targetObjectId = null;
   150→    this.pendingAction  = null;
   151→
   152→    // Fallback/re-routing: counts down; engine updates talk route when <= 0
   153→    this._talkRetargetTimer = 0;
   154→
   155→    // Talk targeting — set by AIEngine when walking to meet another character
   156→    this.pendingTalkTarget   = null;  // Character ref awaiting arrival
   157→    this.pendingTalkDialogue = null;  // What A will say when conversation starts
   158→    this.pendingTalkResponse = null;  // What B will say when conversation starts
   159→
   160→    // Active conversation state
   161→    this.talkTimer    = 0;
   162→    this.talkTimerMax = 0;
   163→    this.talkTarget   = null;  // Character ref of current conversation partner
   164→  }
   165→
   166→  // ── Computed pixel position (Phaser setOrigin(0.5, 1) — feet at py) ─────────
   167→
   168→  get px() {
   169→    if (this.path.length === 0) {
   170→      return this.tx * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   171→    }
   172→    const next = this.path[0];
   173→    return (this.prevTx + (next.tx - this.prevTx) * this.moveProgress) * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   174→  }
   175→
   176→  get py() {
   177→    if (this.path.length === 0) {
   178→      return (this.ty + 1) * TILE_SIZE;
   179→    }
   180→    const next = this.path[0];
   181→    return (this.prevTy + (next.ty - this.prevTy) * this.moveProgress + 1) * TILE_SIZE;
   182→  }
   183→
   184→  // ── Movement ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   185→
   186→  moveTo(goalTx, goalTy) {
   187→    const sx = Math.round(this.tx);
   188→    const sy = Math.round(this.ty);
   189→    const path = findPath(this.walkable, this.gridCols, this.gridRows, sx, sy, goalTx, goalTy);
   190→
   191→    if (path && path.length > 0) {
   192→      this.path         = path;
   193→      this.prevTx       = sx;
   194→      this.prevTy       = sy;
   195→      this.moveProgress = 0;
   196→      this.action       = 'walking';
   197→
   198→      // Set initial facing from first step
   199→      this._updateFacingFromNextTile();
   200→      this._playWalkAnim();
   201→      return true;
   202→    }
   203→    return false;
   204→  }
   205→
   206→  /** Convenience wrapper — start interaction with a named object. */
   207→  startInteraction(objectId, durationMs) {
   208→    this.startInteract(objectId, durationMs);
   209→  }
   210→
   211→  startInteract(target, durationMs) {
   212→    this.action           = 'interacting';
   213→    this.interactTarget   = target;
   214→    this.interactTimer    = durationMs;
   215→    this.interactTimerMax = durationMs;
   216→    if (this.sprite) {
   217→      this.sprite.play(`${this.name}_idle_anim`, true);
   218→    }
   219→  }
   220→
   221→  /** Enter a shared talking state with `partner` for `durationMs` milliseconds. */
   222→  startTalk(partner, durationMs) {
   223→    // Stop any current movement
   224→    this.path        = [];
   225→    this.moveProgress = 0;
   226→
   227→    this.action       = 'talking';
   228→    this.talkTarget   = partner;
   229→    this.talkTimer    = durationMs;
   230→    this.talkTimerMax = durationMs;
   231→
   232→    // Clear any pending object interaction targeting
   233→    this.targetObjectId      = null;
   234→    this.pendingAction       = null;
   235→    // Clear any pending talk targeting (e.g. B was also walking to someone)
   236→    this.pendingTalkTarget   = null;
   237→    this.pendingTalkDialogue = null;
   238→    this.pendingTalkResponse = null;
   239→
   240→    if (this.sprite) {
   241→      this.sprite.play(`${this.name}_idle_anim`, true);
   242→    }
   243→  }
   244→
   245→  // ── Per-frame update ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   246→
   247→  update(deltaMs) {
   248→    if (this.action === 'walking' && this.path.length > 0) {
   249→      const tileDurationMs = 1000 / this.moveSpeed;
   250→      this.moveProgress += deltaMs / tileDurationMs;
   251→
   252→      // Update facing toward next tile in path
   253→      this._updateFacingFromNextTile();
   254→
   255→      // Advance tiles
   256→      while (this.moveProgress >= 1 && this.path.length > 0) {
   257→        this.moveProgress -= 1;
   258→        const arrived = this.path.shift();
   259→        this.prevTx = arrived.tx;
   260→        this.prevTy = arrived.ty;
   261→        this.tx     = arrived.tx;
   262→        this.ty     = arrived.ty;
   263→      }
   264→
   265→      if (this.path.length === 0) {
   266→        this.moveProgress = 0;
   267→        this.action       = 'idle';
   268→        this.wanderTimer  = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   269→        this._playAnim('idle');
   270→      } else {
   271→        this._playWalkAnim();
   272→      }
   273→    } else if (this.action === 'idle') {
   274→      this.wanderTimer -= deltaMs;
   275→    } else if (this.action === 'interacting') {
   276→      this.interactTimer -= deltaMs;
   277→      if (this.interactTimer <= 0) {
   278→        this.action        = 'idle';
   279→        this.interactTarget = null;
   280→        this.wanderTimer   = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   281→        this._playAnim('idle');
   282→      }
   283→    } else if (this.action === 'talking') {
   284→      this.talkTimer -= deltaMs;
   285→      if (this.talkTimer <= 0) {
   286→        this.action      = 'idle';
   287→        this.talkTarget  = null;
   288→        this.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   289→        this._playAnim('idle');
   290→      }
   291→    }
   292→
   293→    // Tick dialogue
   294→    if (this.dialogueTimer > 0) {
   295→      this.dialogueTimer -= deltaMs;
   296→      if (this.dialogueTimer <= 0) this.currentDialogue = null;
   297→    }
   298→
   299→    // Sync Phaser sprite
   300→    if (this.sprite) {
   301→      this.sprite.x = this.px;
   302→      this.sprite.y = this.py;
   303→    }
   304→
   305→    if (this.nameLabel && this.sprite) {
   306→      this.nameLabel.setPosition(this.sprite.x, this.sprite.y - 100);
   307→    }
   308→  }
   309→
   310→  // ── Perception ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   311→
   312→  /** Returns objects within `radius` tiles. */
   313→  getPerceivedObjects(objects, radius = 4) {
   314→    return objects.filter(obj => {
   315→      const dx = obj.tx - this.tx;
   316→      const dy = obj.ty - this.ty;
   317→      return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= radius;
   318→    });
   319→  }
   320→
   321→  // ── Animation helpers ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   322→
   323→  _updateFacingFromNextTile() {
   324→    if (this.path.length === 0) return;
   325→    const next = this.path[0];
   326→    const dx   = next.tx - this.tx;
   327→    const dy   = next.ty - this.ty;
   328→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) {
   329→      this.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'right' : 'left';
   330→    } else {
   331→      this.facing = dy > 0 ? 'down' : 'up';
   332→    }
   333→  }
   334→
   335→  _playAnim(type) {
   336→    if (!this.sprite) return;
   337→    const key = type === 'idle'
   338→      ? `${this.name}_idle_anim`
   339→      : `${this.name}_walk_${this.facing}`;
   340→    if (this.sprite.anims.currentAnim?.key !== key) {
   341→      this.sprite.play(key, true);
   342→    }
   343→    this.sprite.flipX = (type === 'walk' && this.facing === 'left');
   344→  }
   345→
   346→  _playWalkAnim() {
   347→    this._playAnim('walk');
   348→  }
   349→}
   350→

    47→function buildWalkableGrid() {
    48→  const grid = [];
    49→  for (let row = 0; row < GRID_ROWS; row++) {
    50→    const r = [];
    51→    for (let col = 0; col < GRID_COLS; col++) {
    52→      r.push(col >= 1 && col <= 17 && row >= 2 && row <= 9);
    53→    }
    54→    grid.push(r);
    55→  }
    56→  // Mark tiles occupied by objects as non-walkable
    57→  for (const def of OBJECT_DEFS) {
    58→    const { tx, ty } = def.position;
    59→    if (ty >= 0 && ty < GRID_ROWS && tx >= 0 && tx < GRID_COLS) {
    60→      grid[ty][tx] = false;
    61→    }
    62→  }
    63→  return grid;
    64→}

   216→// ── ObjectInstance ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   217→
   218→class ObjectInstance {
   219→  constructor(def) {
   220→    this.id        = def.id;
   221→    this.name      = def.name;
   222→    this.label     = def.name;           // compat for AIEngine
   223→    this.position  = def.position;
   224→    this.tx        = def.position.tx;    // compat for AIEngine distance checks
   225→    this.ty        = def.position.ty;
   226→    this.states    = def.states;
   227→    this.state     = def.state || 'idle';
   228→    this.interactMs = def.interactMs || 8000;
   229→    this.autoTimer = 0;
   230→    this._resetAutoTimer();
   231→
   232→    // Slot system
   233→    this.capacity      = def.capacity ?? 1;
   234→    this._reservations = new Set(); // charNames walking toward this object
   235→    this._occupants    = new Set(); // charNames actively interacting
   236→  }
   237→
   238→  /** True if no more slots are available (reserved + occupied >= capacity). */
   239→  isFull() {
   240→    return this._reservations.size + this._occupants.size >= this.capacity;
   241→  }
   242→
   243→  /**
   244→   * Reserve a slot for charName before they start walking.
   245→   * Returns true if the reservation succeeded, false if the object is full.
   246→   */
   247→  reserve(charName) {
   248→    if (this.isFull()) return false;
   249→    this._reservations.add(charName);
   250→    return true;
   251→  }
   252→
   253→  /**
   254→   * Called when charName arrives at the object.
   255→   * Converts the reservation to an active occupancy.
   256→   */
   257→  arrive(charName) {
   258→    this._reservations.delete(charName);
   259→    this._occupants.add(charName);
   260→  }
   261→
   262→  /**
   263→   * Release a slot when the character finishes interacting or abandons the walk.
   264→   * Warns if charName was not a known occupant or reservation — signals an orphaned slot.
   265→   */
   266→  release(charName) {
   267→    if (!this._reservations.has(charName) && !this._occupants.has(charName)) {
   268→      console.warn(
   269→        `[objects] release('${this.id}', '${charName}'): ` +
   270→        `not a known occupant or reservation — possible orphaned slot`
   271→      );
   272→    }
   273→    this._reservations.delete(charName);
   274→    this._occupants.delete(charName);
   275→  }
   276→
   277→  /** Returns the names of characters who have reserved a slot (walking toward this object). */
   278→  getReservations() { return Array.from(this._reservations); }
   279→
   280→  /** Returns the names of characters who are actively occupying a slot. */
   281→  getOccupants() { return Array.from(this._occupants); }
   282→
   283→  /** Clear all reservations and occupancies (used on sim reset). */
   284→  clearSlots() {
   285→    this._reservations.clear();
   286→    this._occupants.clear();
   287→  }
   288→
   289→  /**
   290→   * Returns current slot occupancy info.
   291→   * @returns {{ capacity, reserved, occupied, available }}
   292→   */
   293→  getSlotInfo() {
   294→    return {
   295→      capacity:  this.capacity,
   296→      reserved:  this._reservations.size,
   297→      occupied:  this._occupants.size,
   298→      available: this.capacity - this._reservations.size - this._occupants.size,
   299→    };
   300→  }
   301→
   302→  _resetAutoTimer() {
   303→    const s = this.states[this.state];
   304→    this.autoTimer = s?.auto_next ? s.auto_next.after * 1000 : 0;
   305→  }
   306→
   307→  /**
   308→   * Trigger an interaction action (e.g. 'use').
   309→   * @returns {{ objectId, state, speech, emoji }|null}
   310→   */
   311→  interact(action = 'use') {
   312→    const s  = this.states[this.state];
   313→    const tr = s?.transitions?.[action];
   314→    if (!tr) return null;
   315→
   316→    this.state = tr.next;
   317→    this._resetAutoTimer();
   318→
   319→    const ns = this.states[this.state];
   320→    return {
   321→      objectId: this.id,
   322→      state:    this.state,
   323→      speech:   ns?.speech || null,
   324→      emoji:    ns?.emoji  || null,
   325→    };
   326→  }
   327→
   328→  /**
   329→   * Advance auto_next timers.
   330→   * @returns {{ objectId, state, emoji, auto: true }|null}
   331→   */
   332→  tick(deltaMs) {
   333→    if (this.autoTimer <= 0) return null;
   334→
   335→    this.autoTimer -= deltaMs;
   336→    if (this.autoTimer > 0) return null;
   337→
   338→    const s = this.states[this.state];
   339→    if (!s?.auto_next) return null;
   340→
   341→    this.state = s.auto_next.state;
   342→    this._resetAutoTimer();
   343→
   344→    const ns = this.states[this.state];
   345→    return {
   346→      objectId: this.id,
   347→      state:    this.state,
   348→      emoji:    ns?.emoji || null,
   349→      auto:     true,
   350→    };
   351→  }
   352→}
   353→
   354→// ── ObjectEngine ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   355→
   356→export class ObjectEngine {
   357→  constructor() {
   358→    this._map = new Map(); // id → ObjectInstance
   359→  }
   360→
   361→  addObjects(defs) {
   362→    for (const def of defs) {
   363→      this._map.set(def.id, new ObjectInstance(def));
   364→    }
   365→  }
   366→
   367→  /**
   368→   * Tick all object timers. Returns any events that fired this frame.
   369→   * @returns {Array<{ objectId, state, emoji, auto }>}
   370→   */
   371→  tick(deltaMs) {
   372→    const events = [];
   373→    for (const obj of this._map.values()) {
   374→      const ev = obj.tick(deltaMs);
   375→      if (ev) events.push(ev);
   376→    }
   377→    return events;
   378→  }
   379→
   380→  /**
   381→   * Trigger an action on an object (e.g. 'use').
   382→   * @returns {{ objectId, state, speech, emoji }|null}
   383→   */
   384→  interact(objectId, action = 'use') {
   385→    return this._map.get(objectId)?.interact(action) ?? null;
   386→  }
   387→
   388→  getAll()    { return Array.from(this._map.values()); }
   389→  getById(id) { return this._map.get(id) ?? null; }
   390→
   391→  reserve(objectId, charName) { return this._map.get(objectId)?.reserve(charName) ?? false; }
   392→  arrive(objectId, charName)  { this._map.get(objectId)?.arrive(charName); }
   393→  release(objectId, charName) { this._map.get(objectId)?.release(charName); }
   394→  clearSlots(objectId)        { this._map.get(objectId)?.clearSlots(); }
   395→  clearAllSlots()             { for (const obj of this._map.values()) obj.clearSlots(); }
   396→}

     1→# AI Aquarium — Café Setting Spec
     2→
     3→## Vision
     4→A cozy café scene where 3 AI characters live their daily routines. Think "lofi girl" stream — small space, rich details, warm vibes. Users watch AI characters make coffee, read books, cook, chat, and go about their day.
     5→
     6→## Critical Visual Rules
     7→
     8→**This is ONE indoor building.** Two floors of the same structure. There must be NO outdoor elements (grass, dirt, sky) between or around the floors. The only outdoor element is a small sidewalk/entrance at the very bottom edge (1-2 tile rows max).
     9→
    10→### Floor/Ceiling Transitions
    11→- Floors are separated by a **ceiling/floor slab** — a thin horizontal band (1-2 tiles) of dark wood or concrete. NOT grass. NOT sky.
    12→- The slab should read as "the ceiling of the café / floor of the apartment."
    13→- Stairs visually connect through this slab.
    14→
    15→### Wall Materials
    16→- **Café walls:** Warm cream/beige plaster with wood wainscoting (bottom half darker wood, top half lighter). Think European coffee shop.
    17→- **Apartment walls:** Warm wood paneling (already looks decent in current build).
    18→- **NO striped/awning patterns** on interior walls.
    19→
    20→### Floor Materials
    21→- **Café floor:** Warm wood planks OR checkerboard tile — but only in the seating area. Behind the counter should be darker wood or stone (staff area).
    22→- **Apartment floor:** Wood planks (darker than café).
    23→
    24→### Density & Coziness
    25→- **No large empty spaces.** Every 3x3 area should have at least one piece of furniture, decoration, or prop.
    26→- **Furniture grouping:** Chairs are ALWAYS next to tables. No lone chairs floating in space.
    27→- **Wall decorations:** Every wall segment longer than 3 tiles should have something on it (art, shelf, menu board, hanging plant, clock, window).
    28→- **Floor decorations:** Rugs under seating clusters, potted plants in corners, small items on tables (cups, books, plates).
    29→
    30→### Size Target
    31→- Total map: roughly 20 wide × 28 tall tiles (including both floors + slab between)
    32→- Ground floor café: ~20×12
    33→- Ceiling slab: ~20×2

   106→

   108→```
   109→idle → brewing (Maple starts) → done (cup appears) → idle (cup taken)
   110→```
   111→
   112→### Display Case

   115→```
   116→

   119→blank → sketching (Nyx draws) → painting (Nyx paints) → finished → blank
   120→```
   121→
   122→### Stove (upstairs)
   123→```
   124→off → heating (Nyx cooks) → cooking (steam particles) → done (food ready) → off
   125→```
   126→
   127→### Book (Sol's)
   128→```
   129→closed → reading (Sol reads, page turn animation) → closed
   130→```
   131→
   132→## AI Decision Format
   133→Characters send perception to LLM, get back:
   134→```json
   135→{
   136→  "action": "interact|move|talk",
   137→  "target": "espresso_machine|sol|upstairs",
   138→  "description": "Makes a latte for Sol",
   139→  "dialogue": "Your usual? Coming right up!"
   140→}
   141→```
   142→
   143→## Visible Feedback Loop
   144→1. AI decides → character walks to target
   145→2. Character arrives → interaction animation plays
   146→3. Object state changes → particles/effects
   147→4. If dialogue → speech bubble appears
   148→5. Other characters react → creates chain of interactions
   149→
   150→## Atmosphere

     1→/**
     2→ * Engine.js — SimulationEngine: manages characters, object state machines, and
     3→ * default random-wander behaviour (with 30% chance of object interaction).
     4→ */
     5→
     6→import { ObjectEngine, OBJECT_DEFS } from './objects.js';
     7→
     8→export class SimulationEngine {
     9→  /**
    10→   * @param {object}      config
    11→   * @param {boolean[][]} config.walkable   - walkable[row][col]
    12→   * @param {number}      config.gridCols
    13→   * @param {number}      config.gridRows
    14→   * @param {object}      [config.aiEngine] - AIEngine instance (optional)
    15→   */
    16→  constructor(config = {}) {
    17→    this.walkable  = config.walkable  || [];
    18→    this.gridCols  = config.gridCols  || 19;
    19→    this.gridRows  = config.gridRows  || 13;
    20→    this.aiEngine  = config.aiEngine  || null;
    21→
    22→    this.characters = [];
    23→
    24→    // Object state machine engine — pre-loaded with Japanese Home objects
    25→    this.objectEngine = new ObjectEngine();
    26→    this.objectEngine.addObjects(OBJECT_DEFS);
    27→
    28→    // Events queued for scene to consume (emoji floats, etc.)
    29→    this.pendingEvents = [];
    30→
    31→    // Sim clock — starts at 08:00 AM game-time
    32→    this.simTimeMs = 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
    33→    // 1 real second = 60 sim seconds  (1 real min = 1 sim hour)
    34→    this.simSpeed  = 60;
    35→
    36→    // Cache walkable tiles list (built lazily)
    37→    this._walkableTiles = null;
    38→  }
    39→
    40→  addCharacter(char) {
    41→    this.characters.push(char);
    42→  }
    43→
    44→  // ── Main update loop ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    45→
    46→  update(deltaMs) {
    47→    // Advance sim clock
    48→    this.simTimeMs += deltaMs * this.simSpeed;
    49→
    50→    // Optional AI decisions — pass live object list so AI sees current states
    51→    if (this.aiEngine) {
    52→      this.aiEngine.update(deltaMs, this.characters, this.objectEngine.getAll(), {
    53→        timeString: this.getSimTimeString(),
    54→        findAdjacentWalkable: this._findAdjacentWalkable.bind(this),
    55→        pushEvent: (ev) => this.pendingEvents.push(ev),
    56→      });
    57→    }
    58→
    59→    // Tick object state machines; collect auto-transition events
    60→    const objEvents = this.objectEngine.tick(deltaMs);
    61→    for (const ev of objEvents) {
    62→      if (ev.emoji) this.pendingEvents.push(ev);
    63→    }
    64→
    65→    for (const char of this.characters) {
    66→      // Defensive release: if interactTarget is set but the character is no longer
    67→      // interacting, an external change (e.g. a stale async AI decision resolving
    68→      // between frames) moved them out of 'interacting' without triggering the
    69→      // normal detection below.  Release the slot now so the object doesn't stay
    70→      // permanently full.
    71→      if (char.interactTarget && char.action !== 'interacting') {
    72→        console.warn(
    73→          `[Engine] defensive release: ${char.name} has interactTarget ` +
    74→          `'${char.interactTarget}' but action='${char.action}' — releasing slot`
    75→        );
    76→        this.objectEngine.release(char.interactTarget, char.name);
    77→        char.interactTarget = null;
    78→      }
    79→
    80→      // Save pre-update state to detect interaction-end transitions
    81→      const prevAction         = char.action;
    82→      const prevInteractTarget = char.interactTarget;
    83→
    84→      // Handle arrival: character reached target object tile
    85→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.targetObjectId) {
    86→        this._handleObjectArrival(char);
    87→      }
    88→
    89→      // Handle arrival: character reached talk target
    90→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.pendingTalkTarget) {
    91→        this._handleTalkArrival(char);
    92→      }
    93→
    94→      // Mid-walk: periodically re-route toward a moving talk target
    95→      if (char.action === 'walking' && char.pendingTalkTarget) {
    96→        char._talkRetargetTimer -= deltaMs;
    97→        if (char._talkRetargetTimer <= 0) {
    98→          char._talkRetargetTimer = 2000; // re-check every 2 s
    99→          this._updateTalkRoute(char);
   100→        }
   101→      }
   102→
   103→      // Trigger random wander (or object visit) when idle and timer expired
   104→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.wanderTimer <= 0) {
   105→        this._doWander(char);
   106→      }
   107→
   108→      // Tick speech timer — fire a random line when it expires
   109→      if (char.dialogue.length > 0 && char.pendingSpeech === null) {
   110→        char.speechTimer -= deltaMs;
   111→        if (char.speechTimer <= 0) {
   112→          const idx = Math.floor(Math.random() * char.dialogue.length);
   113→          char.pendingSpeech = char.dialogue[idx];
   114→          char.speechTimer   = 20000 + Math.random() * 20000; // reset 20–40 s
   115→        }
   116→      }
   117→
   118→      // Per-character update (movement, animations, sprite sync)
   119→      char.update(deltaMs);
   120→
   121→      // Detect interaction end: release slot so other characters can use the object
   122→      if (prevAction === 'interacting' && char.action !== 'interacting' && prevInteractTarget) {
   123→        this.objectEngine.release(prevInteractTarget, char.name);
   124→      }
   125→    }
   126→  }
   127→
   128→  // ── Object interaction ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   129→
   130→  /**
   131→   * Called when a character arrives at an object's adjacent tile.
   132→   * Fires the 'use' transition and puts the character into 'interacting' state.
   133→   * If the object has no valid transition, finds an alternative instead of idling.
   134→   */
   135→  _handleObjectArrival(char) {
   136→    const objectId = char.targetObjectId;
   137→    const action   = char.pendingAction || 'use';
   138→
   139→    // Clear targeting immediately so we don't re-fire on the next idle frame.
   140→    // _fallbackToAlternativeObject may set a new targetObjectId if it finds one.
   141→    char.targetObjectId = null;
   142→    char.pendingAction  = null;
   143→
   144→    const event = this.objectEngine.interact(objectId, action);
   145→
   146→    if (event) {
   147→      // Convert reservation → active occupancy
   148→      this.objectEngine.arrive(objectId, char.name);
   149→
   150→      const obj = this.objectEngine.getById(objectId);
   151→
   152→      // Hold the character for the full auto_next duration if the new state has one;
   153→      // otherwise fall back to the object's generic interactMs.
   154→      let holdMs = obj ? obj.interactMs : 8000;
   155→      if (obj && event.state) {
   156→        const stateDef = obj.states[event.state];
   157→        if (stateDef?.auto_next?.after) {
   158→          holdMs = stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000;
   159→        }
   160→      }
   161→
   162→      // Face toward the object tile before entering interaction
   163→      if (obj) {
   164→        const dx = obj.tx - Math.round(char.tx);
   165→        const dy = obj.ty - Math.round(char.ty);
   166→        if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) {
   167→          char.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'right' : 'left';
   168→        } else {
   169→          char.facing = dy >= 0 ? 'down' : 'up';
   170→        }
   171→      }
   172→
   173→      char.startInteraction(objectId, holdMs);
   174→
   175→      if (event.speech) char.pendingSpeech = event.speech;
   176→      if (event.emoji)  this.pendingEvents.push(event);
   177→    } else {
   178→      // No valid transition (object changed state mid-walk) — release the
   179→      // reservation and try to find an alternative object.
   180→      this.objectEngine.release(objectId, char.name);
   181→      this._fallbackToAlternativeObject(char, objectId);
   182→    }
   183→  }
   184→
   185→  // ── Talk handshake ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   186→
   187→  /**
   188→   * Called when a character arrives at the tile adjacent to their talk target.
   189→   * Checks proximity and re-evaluates B's availability before starting conversation.
   190→   */
   191→  _handleTalkArrival(char) {
   192→    const target = char.pendingTalkTarget;
   193→    char.pendingTalkTarget = null;
   194→
   195→    // Proximity check: target may have moved significantly during the walk.
   196→    const dx   = Math.round(target.tx) - Math.round(char.tx);
   197→    const dy   = Math.round(target.ty) - Math.round(char.ty);
   198→    const dist = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
   199→
   200→    if (dist > 3) {
   201→      // Target has drifted — try to follow if not too far
   202→      if (dist <= 10) {
   203→        const adjTile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(Math.round(target.tx), Math.round(target.ty));
   204→        if (adjTile && char.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {
   205→          // Re-attach pending talk so we retry on next arrival
   206→          char.pendingTalkTarget   = target;
   207→          char._talkRetargetTimer  = 2000;
   208→          return;
   209→        }
   210→      }
   211→      // Too far or unreachable — abort
   212→      this.pendingEvents.push({
   213→        type:      'fallback',
   214→        charLabel: char.label,
   215→        reason:    'talk_target_moved',
   216→        fromLabel: target.label,
   217→        toLabel:   null,
   218→      });
   219→      char.pendingTalkDialogue = null;
   220→      char.pendingTalkResponse = null;
   221→      char.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   222→      return;
   223→    }
   224→
   225→    // Re-check availability: accept if idle or walking, reject if busy
   226→    const canTalk = target.action === 'idle' || target.action === 'walking';
   227→
   228→    if (!canTalk) {
   229→      this.pendingEvents.push({
   230→        type:           'talk_rejected',
   231→        initiatorLabel: char.label,
   232→        targetLabel:    target.label,
   233→      });
   234→      char.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   235→      return;
   236→    }
   237→
   238→    this._startConversation(char, target);
   239→  }
   240→
   241→  /**
   242→   * Configurable conversation duration range (ms).
   243→   * Defaults to 10–15 s; override via constructor config.
   244→   */
   245→  get _talkDurationMs() {
   246→    return 10_000 + Math.random() * 5_000;
   247→  }
   248→
   249→  /**
   250→   * Synchronise charA and charB into a shared 'talking' state.
   251→   * Both face each other, AI timers are paused (via action check in AIEngine),
   252→   * and conversation ends naturally when the timer expires.
   253→   */
   254→  _startConversation(charA, charB) {
   255→    // Release any pending object reservation charB held while walking.
   256→    // startTalk() clears targetObjectId without calling objectEngine.release(),
   257→    // so we must do it here before the slot becomes permanently orphaned.
   258→    if (charB.targetObjectId) {
   259→      this.objectEngine.release(charB.targetObjectId, charB.name);
   260→      charB.targetObjectId = null;
   261→      charB.pendingAction  = null;
   262→    }
   263→
   264→    const duration = this._talkDurationMs;
   265→
   266→    // Face each other
   267→    const dx = Math.round(charB.tx) - Math.round(charA.tx);
   268→    const dy = Math.round(charB.ty) - Math.round(charA.ty);
   269→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) {
   270→      charA.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'right' : 'left';
   271→      charB.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'left'  : 'right';
   272→    } else {
   273→      charA.facing = dy >= 0 ? 'down' : 'up';
   274→      charB.facing = dy >= 0 ? 'up'   : 'down';
   275→    }
   276→
   277→    // Transfer queued dialogue to speech bubbles
   278→    if (charA.pendingTalkDialogue) {
   279→      charA.pendingSpeech          = charA.pendingTalkDialogue;
   280→      charA.pendingTalkDialogue    = null;
   281→    }
   282→    if (charA.pendingTalkResponse) {
   283→      charB.pendingSpeech          = charA.pendingTalkResponse;
   284→      charA.pendingTalkResponse    = null;
   285→    }
   286→
   287→    charA.startTalk(charB, duration);
   288→    charB.startTalk(charA, duration);
   289→
   290→    this.pendingEvents.push({
   291→      type:           'conversation_start',
   292→      initiatorLabel: charA.label,
   293→      targetLabel:    charB.label,
   294→    });
   295→  }
   296→
   297→  // ── Wander ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   298→
   299→  _doWander(char) {
   300→    // 30% chance: walk to a random interactive object instead of wandering freely
   301→    if (Math.random() < 0.3) {
   302→      const objects = this.objectEngine.getAll();
   303→      if (objects.length > 0) {
   304→        // Shuffle and try each until one has an available slot and a reachable adjacent tile
   305→        const shuffled = objects.slice().sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5);
   306→        for (const obj of shuffled) {
   307→          if (obj.isFull()) continue; // skip objects at capacity
   308→          // Only target objects whose current state accepts a 'use' interaction
   309→          const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];
   310→          if (!stateDef?.transitions?.use) continue;
   311→          const tile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(obj.tx, obj.ty);
   312→          if (tile && char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty)) {
   313→            obj.reserve(char.name); // claim a slot before walking
   314→            char.targetObjectId = obj.id;
   315→            char.pendingAction  = 'use';
   316→            return;
   317→          }
   318→        }
   319→        // All objects full/non-interactable/unreachable — fall through to random wander
   320→      }
   321→    }
   322→
   323→    // Random walkable tile
   324→    const tiles = this._getWalkableTiles();
   325→    if (tiles.length === 0) {
   326→      char.wanderTimer = 2000;
   327→      return;
   328→    }
   329→
   330→    const cx = Math.round(char.tx);
   331→    const cy = Math.round(char.ty);
   332→
   333→    let moved = false;
   334→    for (let attempt = 0; attempt < 15; attempt++) {
   335→      const tile = tiles[Math.floor(Math.random() * tiles.length)];
   336→      if (tile.tx === cx && tile.ty === cy) continue;
   337→      moved = char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty);
   338→      if (moved) break;
   339→    }
   340→
   341→    if (!moved) {
   342→      char.wanderTimer = 2000;
   343→    }
   344→  }
   345→
   346→  // ── Fallback helpers ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   347→
   348→  /**
   349→   * Find the closest available object that `char` can interact with right now,
   350→   * excluding the object with `excludeId`.
   351→   * @returns {ObjectInstance|null}
   352→   */
   353→  _findAlternativeObject(char, excludeId) {
   354→    const objects = this.objectEngine.getAll();
   355→    let best     = null;
   356→    let bestDist = Infinity;
   357→
   358→    for (const obj of objects) {
   359→      if (obj.id === excludeId) continue;
   360→      if (obj.isFull()) continue;
   361→      // Require a usable state right now
   362→      const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];
   363→      if (!stateDef?.transitions?.use) continue;
   364→      // Require a reachable adjacent tile
   365→      if (!this._findAdjacentWalkable(obj.tx, obj.ty)) continue;
   366→
   367→      const dx   = obj.tx - Math.round(char.tx);
   368→      const dy   = obj.ty - Math.round(char.ty);
   369→      const dist = dx * dx + dy * dy;
   370→      if (dist < bestDist) { bestDist = dist; best = obj; }
   371→    }
   372→
   373→    return best;
   374→  }
   375→
   376→  /**
   377→   * Called when a character's object interaction fails on arrival.
   378→   * Tries to redirect to the nearest available alternative; emits a 'fallback' event.
   379→   */
   380→  _fallbackToAlternativeObject(char, fromId) {
   381→    const fromObj     = this.objectEngine.getById(fromId);
   382→    const alternative = this._findAlternativeObject(char, fromId);
   383→
   384→    if (alternative) {
   385→      const adjTile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(alternative.tx, alternative.ty);
   386→      if (adjTile && char.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {
   387→        alternative.reserve(char.name);
   388→        char.targetObjectId = alternative.id;
   389→        char.pendingAction  = 'use';
   390→
   391→        this.pendingEvents.push({
   392→          type:      'fallback',
   393→          charLabel: char.label,
   394→          reason:    'object_unavailable',
   395→          fromLabel: fromObj?.name ?? fromId,
   396→          toLabel:   alternative.name,
   397→        });
   398→        return;
   399→      }
   400→    }
   401→
   402→    // No usable alternative — idle
   403→    char.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   404→    this.pendingEvents.push({
   405→      type:      'fallback',
   406→      charLabel: char.label,
   407→      reason:    'object_unavailable',
   408→      fromLabel: fromObj?.name ?? fromId,
   409→      toLabel:   null,
   410→    });
   411→  }
   412→
   413→  /**
   414→   * Called periodically while a character is walking toward a talk target.
   415→   * Re-routes the character if the target has moved, or aborts if too far.
   416→   */
   417→  _updateTalkRoute(char) {
   418→    const target = char.pendingTalkTarget;
   419→    if (!target) return;
   420→
   421→    const dx   = Math.round(target.tx) - Math.round(char.tx);
   422→    const dy   = Math.round(target.ty) - Math.round(char.ty);
   423→    const dist = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
   424→
   425→    // If target has wandered more than 10 tiles away, give up
   426→    if (dist > 10) {
   427→      char.pendingTalkTarget   = null;
   428→      char.pendingTalkDialogue = null;
   429→      char.pendingTalkResponse = null;
   430→      char.path                = [];
   431→      char.action              = 'idle';
   432→      char.wanderTimer         = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   433→
   434→      this.pendingEvents.push({
   435→        type:      'fallback',
   436→        charLabel: char.label,
   437→        reason:    'talk_target_moved',
   438→        fromLabel: target.label,
   439→        toLabel:   null,
   440→      });
   441→      return;
   442→    }
   443→
   444→    // Re-route only if the path end has drifted more than 1 tile from target
   445→    const pathEnd = char.path[char.path.length - 1];
   446→    if (pathEnd) {
   447→      const edx = pathEnd.tx - Math.round(target.tx);
   448→      const edy = pathEnd.ty - Math.round(target.ty);
   449→      if (Math.sqrt(edx * edx + edy * edy) > 1) {
   450→        const adjTile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(Math.round(target.tx), Math.round(target.ty));
   451→        if (adjTile) char.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty);
   452→      }
   453→    }
   454→  }
   455→
   456→  /**
   457→   * Return the first walkable tile cardinally adjacent to (tx, ty), or null.
   458→   */
   459→  _findAdjacentWalkable(tx, ty) {
   460→    const dirs = [
   461→      { tx, ty: ty - 1 },
   462→      { tx, ty: ty + 1 },
   463→      { tx: tx - 1, ty },
   464→      { tx: tx + 1, ty },
   465→    ];
   466→    for (const d of dirs) {
   467→      if (d.tx >= 0 && d.tx < this.gridCols && d.ty >= 0 && d.ty < this.gridRows) {
   468→        if (this.walkable[d.ty]?.[d.tx]) return d;
   469→      }
   470→    }
   471→    return null;
   472→  }
   473→
   474→  _getWalkableTiles() {
   475→    if (this._walkableTiles) return this._walkableTiles;
   476→    const tiles = [];
   477→    for (let row = 0; row < this.gridRows; row++) {
   478→      for (let col = 0; col < this.gridCols; col++) {
   479→        if (this.walkable[row]?.[col]) tiles.push({ tx: col, ty: row });
   480→      }
   481→    }
   482→    this._walkableTiles = tiles;
   483→    return tiles;
   484→  }
   485→
   486→  // ── Sim clock ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   487→
   488→  getSimTimeString() {
   489→    const totalSec = Math.floor(this.simTimeMs / 1000);
   490→    const hours    = Math.floor(totalSec / 3600) % 24;
   491→    const minutes  = Math.floor((totalSec % 3600) / 60);
   492→    const ampm     = hours >= 12 ? 'PM' : 'AM';
   493→    const h        = hours % 12 || 12;
   494→    return `${h}:${String(minutes).padStart(2, '0')} ${ampm}`;
   495→  }
   496→}

The idle animation uses 6 frames, so I'll need to determine how many frames the reading, sitting, and phone animations should have, then generate simple PNG files that match those dimensions.\n\nActually, the better approach is to implement graceful fallbacks in the code itself\u2014I'll set up error handling in the preload phase and check whether animation keys exist before trying to play them, defaulting back to idle if an animation isn't available. This way the code is production-ready even without all the sprite assets in place.\n\nNow I'm noticing the file sizes are surprisingly compressed\u2014that 5KB idle sprite for a 1152x96 image suggests either very simple pixel art or palette-based compression. For placeholder sprites, I could explore generating them programmatically, though that gets complicated without proper image libraries.\n\nActually, the cleaner approach is to reuse the idle spritesheet across all animations by pointing different animation definitions to the same texture key, then swapping in the proper spritesheets later when artists provide them.\n\nThe real constraint here is that the assets don't exist yet\u2014they're marked as \"Available\" but need to be added to the repo alongside the code changes for animation mapping and playback.\n\nFor creating the sprite files, I should check what tools are available\u2014either I can generate simple placeholder PNGs with visual differences (like tinted character variants), or use Python or ImageMagick to create proper test sprites programmatically.",

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #56
Bash TOOL CALL 
{
  "command": "python3 << 'EOF'\n\"\"\"\nGenerate placeholder interaction spritesheets for FRG-243.\nEach sprite is a tinted/modified version of the character's idle sprite.\nFormat: 6 frames, each 48x96 \u2192 total 288x96 pixels.\n\nAnimation types needed:\n- reading: warm orange tint\n- sit: blue tint  \n- sit2: darker blue tint\n- phone: purple/pink tint\n\"\"\"\nfrom PIL import Image, ImageEnhance, ImageFilter\nimport numpy as np\nimport os\n\nCHARS = ['Amelia', 'Lucy', 'Ash']\n# Each interaction anim uses first 6 frames from the idle spritesheet (0-5)\nFRAME_W, FRAME_H = 48, 96\nNUM_FRAMES = 6\nOUT_W = FRAME_W * NUM_FRAMES  # 288\nOUT_H = FRAME_H  # 96\n\n# (anim_name, hue_shift_degrees, saturation_multiplier, brightness_multiplier)\n# We'll use simple color overlays on the non-transparent pixels\nANIM_CONFIGS = {\n    'reading_48x48': (30, 1.4, 1.0),    # warm amber tint\n    'sit_48x48':     (-120, 1.3, 0.95), # cool blue tint\n    'sit2_48x48':    (-150, 1.2, 0.9),  # darker blue-green tint\n    'phone_48x48':   (120, 1.3, 0.95),  # pink/magenta tint\n}\n\ndef apply_color_overlay(arr, hue_shift, sat_mult, bright_mult):\n    \"\"\"Apply a color tint to the non-transparent pixels.\"\"\"\n    from PIL import Image\n    import colorsys\n    \n    result = arr.copy().astype(float)\n    \n    for y in range(arr.shape[0]):\n        for x in range(arr.shape[1]):\n            a = arr[y, x, 3]\n            if a == 0:\n                continue\n            r, g, b = arr[y, x, 0] / 255.0, arr[y, x, 1] / 255.0, arr[y, x, 2] / 255.0\n            h, s, v = colorsys.rgb_to_hsv(r, g, b)\n            # Shift hue\n            h = (h + hue_shift / 360.0) % 1.0\n            # Adjust saturation\n            s = min(1.0, s * sat_mult)\n            # Adjust brightness\n            v = min(1.0, v * bright_mult)\n            r2, g2, b2 = colorsys.hsv_to_rgb(h, s, v)\n            result[y, x, 0] = r2 * 255\n            result[y, x, 1] = g2 * 255\n            result[y, x, 2] = b2 * 255\n    \n    return result.astype(np.uint8)\n\noutput_dir = '/home/gem/project/assets/characters'\n\nfor char_name in CHARS:\n    idle_path = os.path.join(output_dir, f'{char_name}_idle.png')\n    idle_img = Image.open(idle_path)\n    idle_arr = np.array(idle_img)\n    \n    # Extract first 6 frames (288x96 px from the idle spritesheet)\n    # Idle sheet is 1152x96 = 24 frames of 48x96\n    source = idle_arr[:, :OUT_W, :]  # first 288 pixels wide, 6 frames\n    \n    for anim_name, (hue_shift, sat_mult, bright_mult) in ANIM_CONFIGS.items():\n        tinted = apply_color_overlay(source, hue_shift, sat_mult, bright_mult)\n        out_img = Image.fromarray(tinted, 'RGBA')\n        out_path = os.path.join(output_dir, f'{char_name}_{anim_name}.png')\n        out_img.save(out_path, optimize=True)\n        print(f\"Generated: {out_path} ({os.path.getsize(out_path)} bytes)\")\n\nprint(\"Done!\")\nEOF"
}

288\nOUT_H = FRAME_H  # 96\n\n# (anim_name, hue_shift_degrees, saturation_multiplier, brightness_multiplier)\n# We'll use simple color overlays on the non-transparent pixels\nANIM_CONFIGS = {\n    'reading_48x48': (30, 1.4, 1.0),    # warm amber tint\n    'sit_48x48':     (-120, 1.3, 0.95), # cool blue tint\n    'sit2_48x48':    (-150, 1.2, 0.9),  # darker blue-green tint\n    'phone_48x48':   (120, 1.3, 0.95),  # pink/magenta tint\n}\n\ndef apply_color_overlay(arr, hue_shift, sat_mult, bright_mult):\n    \"\"\"Apply a color tint to the non-transparent pixels.\"\"\"\n    from PIL import Image\n    import colorsys\n    \n    result = arr.copy().astype(float)\n    \n    for y in range(arr.shape[0]):\n        for x in range(arr.shape[1]):\n            a = arr[y, x, 3]\n            if a == 0:\n                continue\n            r, g, b = arr[y, x, 0] / 255.0, arr[y, x, 1] / 255.0, arr[y, x, 2] / 255.0\n            h, s, v = colorsys.rgb_to_hsv(r, g, b)\n            # Shift hue\n            h = (h + hue_shift / 360.0) % 1.0\n            # Adjust saturation\n            s = min(1.0, s * sat_mult)\n            # Adjust brightness\n            v = min(1.0, v * bright_mult)\n            r2, g2, b2 = colorsys.hsv_to_rgb(h, s, v)\n            result[y, x, 0] = r2 * 255\n            result[y, x, 1] = g2 * 255\n            result[y, x, 2] = b2 * 255\n    \n    return result.astype(np.uint8)\n\noutput_dir = '/home/gem/project/assets/characters'\n\nfor char_name in CHARS:\n    idle_path = os.path.join(output_dir, f'{char_name}_idle.png')\n    idle_img = Image.open(idle_path)\n    idle_arr = np.array(idle_img)\n    \n    # Extract first 6 frames (288x96 px from the idle spritesheet)\n    # Idle sheet is 1152x96 = 24 frames of 48x96\n    source = idle_arr[:, :OUT_W, :]  # first 288 pixels wide, 6 frames\n    \n    for anim_name, (hue_shift, sat_mult, bright_mult) in ANIM_CONFIGS.items():\n        tinted = apply_color_overlay(source, hue_shift, sat_mult, bright_mult)\n        out_img = Image.fromarray(tinted, 'RGBA')\n        out_path = os.path.join(output_dir, f'{char_name}_{anim_name}.png')\n        out_img.save(out_path, optimize=True)\n        print(f\"Generated: {out_path} ({os.path.getsize(out_path)} bytes)\")\n\nprint(\"Done!\")\nEOF"

   154→      let holdMs = obj ? obj.interactMs : 8000;
   155→      if (obj && event.state) {
   156→        const stateDef = obj.states[event.state];
   157→        if (stateDef?.auto_next?.after) {
   158→          holdMs = stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000;
   159→        }
   160→      }
   161→
   162→      // Face toward the object tile before entering interaction
   163→      if (obj) {
   164→        const dx = obj.tx - Math.round(char.tx);
   165→        const dy = obj.ty - Math.round(char.ty);
   166→        if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) {
   167→          char.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'right' : 'left';
   168→        } else {
   169→          char.facing = dy >= 0 ? 'down' : 'up';
   170→        }
   171→      }
   172→
   173→      char.startInteraction(objectId, holdMs, obj?.interactAnim ?? null);
   174→
   175→      if (event.speech) char.pendingSpeech = event.speech;
   176→      if (event.emoji)  this.pendingEvents.push(event);
   177→    } else {
   178→      // No valid transition (object changed state mid-walk) — release the
   179→      // reservation and try to find an alternative object.

USERMESSAGE #152
✓ TOOL RESULT
SUCCESS 
{"id":"ddf62c48-94a0-40cd-9a7a-cdc23aabc2af","identifier":"FRG-243","title":"Characters play contextual animations during interactions","description":"## Problem

Characters play idle_anim during all interactions. Sol reads a bookshelf but stands frozen. Maple uses the stove but looks like she is just standing there.

## Available Assets (48x48 LimeZu sprites)

All 3 characters (Amelia/Lucy/Ash) have:

* reading_48x48.png — for bookshelf, desk
* sit_48x48.png / sit2 / sit3 — for kotatsu, TV, bed
* phone_48x48.png — general interaction fallback

## What to do

1. Map each object to an interaction animation: bookshelf->reading, desk->reading, kotatsu->sit, tv->sit, bed->sit2, stove->phone, fridge->phone, tea_set->phone, easel->phone, bonsai->phone
2. Load these spritesheets in scene.js
3. In startInteract(), play the mapped animation instead of idle_anim
4. On interaction end, return to idle_anim

## Acceptance Criteria

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #155
## Status DONE ## What Changed - `src/objects.js` — Added `interactAnim` field to all 10 object definitions (reading/sit/sit2/phone) and exposed `interactAnim` from `ObjectInstance` constructor - `src/scene.js` — Load 4 interaction spritesheet types per character in `preload()`; register `${name}_interact_${type}` Phaser animation keys in `create()` - `src/Character.js` — `startInteract()` / `startInteraction()` now accept optional `animType`, look up `${name}_interact_${animType}` and fall back to `idle_anim` if the key doesn't exist - `src/Engine.js` — Pass `obj.interactAnim` to `startInteraction()` on object arrival - `assets/characters/{Amelia,Lucy,Ash}_{reading,sit,sit2,phone}_48x48.png` — Placeholder spritesheets (tinted idle frames, 288×96 px, 6 frames) so the game runs immediately; replace with final LimeZu art ## Key Decisions - **Graceful fallback**: `Character.js` checks `this.sprite.anims.exists(key)` before playing — missing assets won't crash the game, they silently fall back to idle - **Placeholder sprites via PIL**: Created tinted variants of the idle sprite (amber=reading, blue=sit, dark-blue=sit2, pink=phone) so QA can visually distinguish animation states while waiting for final art - **`interactAnim` lives on the object def**: Keeping the animation type co-located with the object definition (in `objects.js`) is the natural place — no cross-file mapping table needed ## PR / Branch - Branch: `feature/FRG-243-contextual-interaction-animations` - PR: https://github.com/chillkimtest-oss/ai-aquarium-phaser/pull/15
